The hotel is built with the essence of Italian Byzantine architecture and the tone of Chinese minimalism and classicism.
No matter what room type you choose here, you can enjoy the oversized silent floor-to-ceiling viewing windows.
The hotel's breakfast is a Chinese and Western buffet on the first floor. There are not many types, but they are all exquisite and taste good.
The hotel also has charging parking spaces, which solves our battery life anxiety when traveling.
The 3rd floor of the hotel is the SPA and gym. We didn't experience the SPA because of the time, but the environment is very comfortable after looking at it.
In addition, there is an executive bar on the top floor of the hotel by the river, where you can enjoy Italian afternoon tea and coffee while enjoying the river view.
For those who want to travel to Guilin and want to live in style, it is right to come to CIAO~
